  68ZN CG           The authors present data for energies up to 2418 with an     
  68ZN2CG anti-COMPTON GELI system normalized to IG(1077)=1000 and data for      
  68ZN3CG EG>2200 measured with a pair spectrometer and separately normalized    
  68ZN4CG to IG(6910)=1000. The low-energy data are here presented normalized    
  68ZN5CG to IG(1077)=100. The conversion factor to get IG per 100 neutron       
  68ZN6CG captures is 0.75 6. The data above 2418G (including the 2303.4 G       
  68ZN7CG not given in the authors' low-energy table) are renormalized to the    
  68ZN8CG low-energy data by choosing IG(6910)=6.0 17. When multiplied by the    
  68ZN9CG above conversion factor, this procedure gives IG(6910)=4.5 13 per      
  68ZNACG 100 neutron captures as determined by the authors. If the overlap      
  68ZNBCG between low and high energy spectra is used, one would get             
  68ZNCCG IG(6910)=4.4 8 relative to IG(1077)=100, a value somewhat smaller than,
  68ZNDCG but consistent with 6.0 17.
